		function genUID() {
			return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
				var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);

			var cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');

			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

			beacon = getCookieValue('wikia_beacon_id'),

		<article id="WikiaMainContent" class="WikiaMainContent">
			<div id="WikiaMainContentContainer" class="WikiaMainContentContainer">
				
													
				
				<div id="WikiaArticle" class="WikiaArticle">
					<div class="home-top-right-ads">
										</div>

					
					<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr mw-content-text"><!-- Google Tag Manager (noscript) --><noscript><iframe src="https://www.googletagmanager.com/ns.html?id=GTM-MDPTN53" height="0" width="0" style="display:none;visibility:hidden"></iframe></noscript><!-- End Google Tag Manager (noscript) --><p><a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Civilization VI"  	 	><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/0/0b/BackArrowGreen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20130127010918" 	 alt="BackArrowGreen"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="BackArrowGreen.png" 	data-image-name="BackArrowGreen.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="17"  	 	 	 	></a> <a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI" title="Civilization VI">Back to Civilization VI</a><br />
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/a/ad/Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28Civ6%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161022012426" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Steam trading card large Theodore Roosevelt (Civ6)"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28Civ6%29.jpg" 	data-image-name="Steam trading card large Theodore Roosevelt (Civ6).jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/a/ad/Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28Civ6%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161022012426"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/a/ad/Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28Civ6%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161022012426" 	 alt="Steam trading card large Theodore Roosevelt (Civ6)"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28Civ6%29.jpg" 	data-image-name="Steam trading card large Theodore Roosevelt (Civ6).jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Steam_trading_card_large_Theodore_Roosevelt_(Civ6).jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Theodore Roosevelt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><b>Leaders</b> are symbolic representatives of the playable <a href="/wiki/Civilizations_(Civ6)" title="Civilizations (Civ6)">civilizations</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI" title="Civilization VI">Civilization VI</a></i>. They are based on historical figures who accomplished great things or successfully led their people through periods of adversity.
</p><p>Each leader has both a unique ability (which gives him or her special bonuses and gameplay advantages) and an <a href="/wiki/Agenda_(Civ6)" title="Agenda (Civ6)">agenda</a> (which affects how he or she plays the game and interacts with other players when controlled by the <a href="/wiki/AI" title="AI">AI</a>). Some leaders' unique abilities allow them to unlock <a href="/wiki/Unique_unit_(Civ6)" title="Unique unit (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">unique units</a>, <a href="/wiki/Buildings_(Civ6)" title="Buildings (Civ6)">buildings</a> or <a href="/wiki/Tile_improvement_(Civ6)" title="Tile improvement (Civ6)">tile improvements</a> after researching specific <a href="/wiki/Technologies_(Civ6)" title="Technologies (Civ6)">technologies</a> or <a href="/wiki/Civics_(Civ6)" title="Civics (Civ6)">civics</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Vanilla" title="Vanilla">vanilla</a> <i>Civilization VI</i>, there is one leader for each civilization (except the <a href="/wiki/Greek_(Civ6)" title="Greek (Civ6)">Greeks</a>). The <i><a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI:_Rise_and_Fall" title="Civilization VI: Rise and Fall">Rise and Fall</a></i> expansion adds <a href="/wiki/Chandragupta_(Civ6)" title="Chandragupta (Civ6)">Chandragupta</a> as an <a href="/wiki/Indian_(Civ6)" title="Indian (Civ6)">Indian</a> leader, and the <i><a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI:_Gathering_Storm" title="Civilization VI: Gathering Storm">Gathering Storm</a></i> expansion adds <a href="/wiki/Eleanor_of_Aquitaine_(Civ6)" title="Eleanor of Aquitaine (Civ6)">Eleanor of Aquitaine</a> as an <a href="/wiki/English_(Civ6)" title="English (Civ6)">English</a> and <a href="/wiki/French_(Civ6)" title="French (Civ6)">French</a> leader. As of <i>Gathering Storm</i>, the total number of leaders in the game is 45.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_Leaders">List of Leaders</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Leaders_(Civ6)?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit List of Leaders section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable sortable">
<tr>
<th>Leader
</th><th>Civilization
</th><th>Leader Ability
</th><th>Leader Agenda
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/Alexander_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Alexander"  	 	><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/3/33/Alexander_%28Civ6%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/44?cb=20180216210702" 	 alt="Alexander (Civ6)"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Alexander_%28Civ6%29.png" 	data-image-name="Alexander (Civ6).png" 	 	 width="44"  	 height="44"  	 	 	 	></a>&#160;<br /><a href="/wiki/Alexander_(Civ6)" title="Alexander (Civ6)">Alexander</a><sup id="cite_ref-:2_0-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-0">[1]</a></sup>
</td><td style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/Macedonian_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Macedonian"  	 	><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/c/ca/Macedonian_%28Civ6%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/44?cb=20190216092204" 	 alt="Macedonian (Civ6)"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Macedonian_%28Civ6%29.png" 	data-image-name="Macedonian (Civ6).png" 	 	 width="44"  	 height="44"  	 	 	 	></a>&#160;<br /><a href="/wiki/Macedonian_(Civ6)" title="Macedonian (Civ6)">Macedonian</a><sup id="cite_ref-:2_0-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-0">[1]</a></sup>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>To the World's End</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Macedonian <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> never incur <a href="/wiki/War_weariness_(Civ6)" title="War weariness (Civ6)">war weariness</a>. All military units heal completely when a city with a <a href="/wiki/Wonder_(Civ6)" title="Wonder (Civ6)">Wonder</a> is captured. Gain the <a href="/wiki/Hetairoi_(Civ6)" title="Hetairoi (Civ6)">Hetairoi</a> unique unit with <a href="/wiki/Horseback_Riding_(Civ6)" title="Horseback Riding (Civ6)">Horseback Riding</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Short Life of Glory</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes civilizations at war with powers other than Macedon. </td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>City Planner</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to keep the maximum number of <a href="/wiki/District_(Civ6)" title="District (Civ6)">districts</a> in each <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">city</a>, and likes those that do the same. Dislikes civilizations that don't build as many districts as possible in their cities.
</p>
</div>

</p>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Queen of the Nile</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes civilizations with powerful militaries, and will try to ally with them to avoid conflict. Dislikes civilizations with weak militaries.
</p>

<p>+2 <a href="/wiki/Movement_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Moves"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6Movement"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6Movement.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6Movement.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/8/89/Civ6Movement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427165924"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/8/89/Civ6Movement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427165924" 	 alt="Civ6Movement"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6Movement.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6Movement.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Movement for all <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)" title="Units (Civ6)">units</a> for the next 10 turns after declaring a <a href="/wiki/Casus_Belli_(Civ6)#Surprise_War" title="Casus Belli (Civ6)">Surprise War</a>. Surprise Wars count as <a href="/wiki/Casus_Belli_(Civ6)#Formal_War" title="Casus Belli (Civ6)">Formal Wars</a> for the purposes of <a href="/wiki/Warmongering_(Civ6)" title="Warmongering (Civ6)">warmongering</a> penalties and <a href="/wiki/War_weariness_(Civ6)" title="War weariness (Civ6)">war weariness</a>. Occupied <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> have no penalties to their yields.

Surprise Wars count as <a href="/wiki/Casus_Belli_(Civ6)#Formal_War" title="Casus Belli (Civ6)">Formal Wars</a> for the purposes of <a href="/wiki/Warmongering_(Civ6)" title="Warmongering (Civ6)">warmongering</a> penalties and <a href="/wiki/War_weariness_(Civ6)" title="War weariness (Civ6)">war weariness</a>. Occupied <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> have no penalties to their yields. +5 <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">Loyalty</a> per turn in occupied cities with a garrisoned unit.

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Opportunist</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Will often declare <a href="/wiki/Casus_Belli_(Civ6)#Surprise_War" title="Casus Belli (Civ6)">Surprise Wars</a>, and likes civilizations that do the same. Dislikes civilizations that don't declare Surprise Wars.

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Court of Love</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Each <a href="/wiki/Great_Work_(Civ6)" title="Great Work (Civ6)">Great Work</a> in her <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> causes foreign cities within 9 tiles to lose 1 <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">Loyalty</a> per turn. Any foreign city that leaves its <a href="/wiki/Civilizations_(Civ6)" title="Civilizations (Civ6)">civilization</a> due to loss of Loyalty and is receiving the most Loyalty pressure from Eleanor instantly joins her empire, instead of becoming a <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)#Free_Cities" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">Free City</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Angevin Empire</b>

<p>Gain an additional Military <a href="/wiki/Policy_Cards_(Civ6)" title="Policy Cards (Civ6)">policy slot</a> in all <a href="/wiki/Government_(Civ6)" title="Government (Civ6)">Governments</a>. +7 <a href="/wiki/Strength_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Strength"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Combat Strength for all units when fighting <a href="/wiki/City-state_(Civ6)" title="City-state (Civ6)">city-states</a> and their units.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Iron Crown</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Will try to conquer as many <a href="/wiki/City-state_(Civ6)" title="City-state (Civ6)">city-states</a> as possible, and likes those who do not associate with them. Dislikes <a href="/wiki/Suzerain_(Civ6)" title="Suzerain (Civ6)">Suzerains</a> of city-states, or civilizations that have conquered city-states.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Adventures of Enkidu</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>May declare war on anyone at war with his <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Alliance" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">allies</a> without incurring <a href="/wiki/Warmongering_(Civ6)" title="Warmongering (Civ6)">warmonger</a> penalties. When at war with a common foe, Sumerian and allied <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)" title="Units (Civ6)">units</a> share <a href="/wiki/Pillage_(Civ6)" title="Pillage (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">pillage</a> rewards and combat experience if within 5 <a href="/wiki/Tile_(Civ6)" title="Tile (Civ6)">tiles</a> of each other.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI:_Rise_and_Fall" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Civilization VI: Rise and Fall"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="R&amp;amp;F-Only"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="R%26F-Only.png" 	data-image-name="R&amp;amp;F-Only.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/d/d0/R%26F-Only.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/28?cb=20181121051626"  	 width="28"  	 height="14"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/d/d0/R%26F-Only.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/28?cb=20181121051626" 	 alt="R&amp;amp;F-Only"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="R%26F-Only.png" 	data-image-name="R&amp;amp;F-Only.png" 	 	 width="28"  	 height="14"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> May declare war on anyone at war with his <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Alliance" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">allies</a> without incurring <a href="/wiki/Warmongering_(Civ6)" title="Warmongering (Civ6)">warmonger</a> penalties. When at war with a common foe, Sumerian and allied <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)" title="Units (Civ6)">units</a> share <a href="/wiki/Pillage_(Civ6)" title="Pillage (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">pillage</a> rewards and combat experience if within 5 <a href="/wiki/Tile_(Civ6)" title="Tile (Civ6)">tiles</a> of each other. Earn <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Alliance" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">Alliance Points</a> per-turn for being at war with a common foe.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Ally of Enkidu</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Is easy to <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Declaring_Friendship" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">befriend</a>, and likes civilizations who are his <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Declaring_Friendship" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">Declared Friends</a>. Dislikes anyone denouncing or attacking his friends.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>With Your Shield Or On It</b>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Thunderbolt of the North</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>+50% <a href="/wiki/Production_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Production"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6Production"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6Production.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6Production.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/7/74/Civ6Production.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200501084523"  	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/7/74/Civ6Production.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200501084523" 	 alt="Civ6Production"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6Production.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6Production.png" 	 	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> <a href="/wiki/Production_(Civ6)" title="Production (Civ6)">Production</a> toward <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)#Naval_Melee" title="Units (Civ6)">naval melee units</a>. All <a href="/wiki/Naval_unit_(Civ6)" title="Naval unit (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">naval</a> melee units gain the ability to perform Coastal Raids. Gain the <a href="/wiki/Viking_Longship_(Civ6)" title="Viking Longship (Civ6)">Viking Longship</a> unique unit with <a href="/wiki/Sailing_(Civ6)" title="Sailing (Civ6)">Sailing</a>.

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Perpetually on Guard</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Forms <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Defensive_Pact" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">Defensive Pacts</a> with friends and likes civilizations that liberate <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a>. Dislikes civilizations that are occupying enemy cities.
</p>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Minerva of the North</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p><a href="/wiki/Building_(Civ6)" title="Building (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">Buildings</a> with at least three <a href="/wiki/Great_Work_(Civ6)" title="Great Work (Civ6)">Great Work</a> slots and <a href="/wiki/Wonder_(Civ6)" title="Wonder (Civ6)">wonders</a> with at least two Great Work slots are automatically <a href="/wiki/Theming_bonus_(Civ6)" title="Theming bonus (Civ6)">themed</a> when all slots are filled. Gains the <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Bibliotheque_(Civ6)" title="Queen's Bibliotheque (Civ6)">Queen's Bibliotheque</a> <a href="/wiki/Buildings_(Civ6)" title="Buildings (Civ6)">unique building</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Government_Plaza_(Civ6)" title="Government Plaza (Civ6)">Government Plaza</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Bibliophile</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to collect as many <a href="/wiki/Great_Work_(Civ6)" title="Great Work (Civ6)">Great Works</a> as possible, and likes those who leave them to her. Dislikes civilizations with many Great Works.
</p>
</div>

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to avoid contributing to climate change by not removing features, planting <a href="/wiki/Woods_(Civ6)" title="Woods (Civ6)">Woods</a>, and founding <a href="/wiki/National_Park_(Civ6)" title="National Park (Civ6)">National Parks</a>, and likes those who do the same. </p>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Ix Mutal Ajaw</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Non-capital cities gain +10% to all yields if within six tiles of the Mayan <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Capital"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812"  	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" title="Capital (Civ6)">Capital</a> <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" title="Capital (Civ6)">capital</a>, and -15% to all yields if more than six tiles away. All units receive +5 <a href="/wiki/Strength_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Strength"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Combat Strength when within six tiles of the Mayan <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Capital"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812"  	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" title="Capital (Civ6)">Capital</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Solitary</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Keeps her cities clustered around her <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Capital"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812"  	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/4/4d/Capital6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20200429094812" 	 alt="Capital6"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Capital6.png" 	data-image-name="Capital6.png" 	 	 width="16"  	 height="16"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> <a href="/wiki/Capital_(Civ6)" title="Capital (Civ6)">Capital</a>, and likes civilizations who settle far away from her. Dislikes those who encroach upon her borders with cities or troops.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Swift Hawk</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Defeating an enemy <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)" title="Units (Civ6)">unit</a> within the borders of an enemy <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">city</a> causes that city to lose 20 <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">Loyalty</a>. Pillaging a <a href="/wiki/Tile_(Civ6)" title="Tile (Civ6)">tile</a> within the borders of an enemy city causes that city to lose 5 Loyalty.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Spirit of Tucapel</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to maintain his cities <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">loyal</a>, and likes civilizations who do the same. Dislikes those that fail to maintain the loyalty of their people.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Religious Convert</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Can't build <a href="/wiki/Holy_Site_(Civ6)" title="Holy Site (Civ6)">Holy Sites</a> or found a <a href="/wiki/Religion_(Civ6)" title="Religion (Civ6)">religion</a>, but receives all the <a href="/wiki/Religion_(Civ6)#Beliefs" title="Religion (Civ6)">beliefs</a> of any religion that has established itself as Kongo's majority religion, not just the <a href="/wiki/Religion_(Civ6)#Beliefs" title="Religion (Civ6)">Follower</a> beliefs. Building a <a href="/wiki/Mbanza_(Civ6)" title="Mbanza (Civ6)">Mbanza</a> or <a href="/wiki/Theater_Square_(Civ6)" title="Theater Square (Civ6)">Theater Square</a> grants a free <a href="/wiki/Apostle_(Civ6)" title="Apostle (Civ6)">Apostle</a> of the city's majority religion.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Enthusiastic Disciple</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes civilizations that bring religion to the Kongo. Dislikes those who have founded a religion but not spread it to a Kongolese city.
</p>
</div>
</td></tr>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Westernizer</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes those that are ahead in <a href="/wiki/Technologies_(Civ6)" title="Technologies (Civ6)">civics</a> and <a href="/wiki/Technologies_(Civ6)" title="Technologies (Civ6)">technologies</a>. Dislikes backwards civilizations that are behind in <a href="/wiki/Civics_(Civ6)" title="Civics (Civ6)">civics</a> and <a href="/wiki/Technologies_(Civ6)" title="Technologies (Civ6)">technologies</a>.
</p>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Counter Reformer</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes civilizations who follow the same Religion as him, and wants his cities to all follow the same Religion. Dislikes those who spread their Religion into his empire.
</p>

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Establishes as many <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Alliance" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">Alliances</a> as possible, and likes those who do the same. Dislikes civilizations that don't establish Alliances.
</p>

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">

</p>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Ayyubid Dynasty</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Wants his <a href="/wiki/Religion_(Civ6)#Worship_Beliefs" title="Religion (Civ6)">Worship</a> building in as many <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> as possible, and likes civilizations with it. Dislikes civilizations following other <a href="/wiki/Religion_(Civ6)" title="Religion (Civ6)">Religions</a> or waging war on followers of his Religion.
</p>
</div>

</p>

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Entering a new <a href="/wiki/Era_(Civ6)" title="Era (Civ6)">era</a> grants a <a href="/wiki/Comandante_General_(Civ6)" title="Comandante General (Civ6)">Comandante General</a>, a unique type of <a href="/wiki/Great_People_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Great Person"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="GreatPerson6"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="GreatPerson6.png" 	data-image-name="GreatPerson6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/9/9a/GreatPerson6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427172032"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/9/9a/GreatPerson6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427172032" 	 alt="GreatPerson6"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="GreatPerson6.png" 	data-image-name="GreatPerson6.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Great Person.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Carabobo</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Focuses on <a href="/wiki/Promotion_(Civ6)" title="Promotion (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">promoting</a> his <a href="/wiki/Units_(Civ6)" title="Units (Civ6)">units</a> by building many <a href="/wiki/Encampment_(Civ6)" title="Encampment (Civ6)">Encampments</a>, and likes civilizations with many promoted units. Dislikes civilizations without an elite, highly-promoted army.
</p>
</div>
</td></tr>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Grand Vizier</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Has access to a unique <a href="/wiki/Governor_(Civ6)" title="Governor (Civ6)">Governor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ibrahim_(Grand_Vizier)_(Civ6)" title="Ibrahim (Grand Vizier) (Civ6)">Ibrahim, the Grand Vizier</a>. Gain the <a href="/wiki/Janissary_(Civ6)" title="Janissary (Civ6)">Janissary</a> <a href="/wiki/Unique_unit_(Civ6)" title="Unique unit (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">unique unit</a> with <a href="/wiki/Gunpowder_(Civ6)" title="Gunpowder (Civ6)">Gunpowder</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Lawgiver</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to keep his <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> <a href="/wiki/Amenities_(Civ6)" title="Amenities (Civ6)">happy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_(Civ6)" title="Loyalty (Civ6)">loyal</a>, and likes those who do the same, especially if they have taken cities from other civilizations. Dislikes those who struggle with happiness and loyalty, or that own few conquered cities.
</p>
</div>

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">

<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>+5 <a href="/wiki/Strength_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Strength"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Combat Strength for all units inside America's home <a href="/wiki/Continent_(Civ6)" title="Continent (Civ6)">continent</a>. +1 <a href="/wiki/Appeal_(Civ6)" title="Appeal (Civ6)">Appeal</a> to all <a href="/wiki/Tile_(Civ6)" title="Tile (Civ6)">tiles</a> in a <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">city</a> with a <a href="/wiki/National_Park_(Civ6)" title="National Park (Civ6)">National Park</a>. Gain the <a href="/wiki/Rough_Rider_(Civ6)" title="Rough Rider (Civ6)">Rough Rider</a> <a href="/wiki/Unique_unit_(Civ6)" title="Unique unit (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">unique unit</a> with <a href="/wiki/Rifling_(Civ6)" title="Rifling (Civ6)">Rifling</a>.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Big Stick Policy</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes peaceful civilizations that have a <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">city</a> on his home <a href="/wiki/Continent_(Civ6)" title="Continent (Civ6)">continent</a>. Dislikes civilizations starting wars on his continent.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Killer of Cyrus</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>All units receive +5 <a href="/wiki/Strength_(Civ6)" 	class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" 	 title="Strength"  	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032"  	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/civilization/images/b/b6/Civ6StrengthIcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/18?cb=20200427170032" 	 alt="Civ6StrengthIcon"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	data-image-name="Civ6StrengthIcon.png" 	 	 width="18"  	 height="18"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a> Combat Strength when attacking wounded units, and heal up to 30 hit points after killing a unit.
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Backstab Averse</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Likes civilizations who are her <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy_(Civ6)#Declaring_Friendship" title="Diplomacy (Civ6)">Declared Friends</a>. Dislikes civilizations who backstab their former allies and declare <a href="/wiki/Casus_Belli_(Civ6)#Surprise_War" title="Casus Belli (Civ6)">Surprise Wars</a>.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Trajan's Column</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>All founded <a href="/wiki/City_(Civ6)" title="City (Civ6)">cities</a> start with a free <a href="/wiki/Building_(Civ6)" title="Building (Civ6)" class="mw-redirect">building</a> in the <a href="/wiki/City_Center_(Civ6)" title="City Center (Civ6)">City Center</a>. (A <a href="/wiki/Monument_(Civ6)" title="Monument (Civ6)">Monument</a> if the game is started in the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Era_(Civ6)" title="Ancient Era (Civ6)">Ancient Era</a>)
</p>
</div>
</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Optimus Princeps</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<p>Tries to include as much territory as possible in his empire, and likes those who do the same. Dislikes civilizations with little territory.
</p>
</div>

</td><td class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" data-expandtext="Expand" data-collapsetext="Collapse"><b>Sun Never Sets</b>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">

</p>
